# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/prometheus/prometheus` — use `repo:^github.com/prometheus/prometheus$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/prometheus/prometheus`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir`

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive analysis of the TLS configuration flow in prometheus/prometheus. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've traced how TLS configuration flows from **prometheus/prometheus** through **prometheus-common** (github.com/prometheus/common/config) to the actual `*tls.Config` and `*http.Client` used in HTTP connections.

### Key Findings:

**Configuration Definition** (config/config.go):
- **ScrapeConfig** - HTTPClientConfig for scrape targets (line 747)
- **RemoteWriteConfig** - HTTPClientConfig for remote write (line 1419)
- **RemoteReadConfig** - HTTPClientConfig for remote read (line 1587)
- **AlertmanagerConfig** - HTTPClientConfig for alertmanager (line 1300)
- **TracingConfig** - Direct TLSConfig field (line 1160)

**Client Creation Paths**:
1. **Scrape**: `scrape/scrape.go` (line 155) → `newScrapeClient()` → `config_util.NewClientFromConfig()`
2. **Remote Write**: `storage/remote/write.go` (line 169) → `NewWriteClient()` → `config_util.NewClientFromConfig()`
3. **Remote Read**: Similar flow through `storage/remote/client.go`
4. **Tracing**: `tracing/tracing.go` (lines 189, 222) → Direct `config_util.NewTLSConfig()`
5. **Discovery**: Multiple modules (triton, openstack, aws, consul, http) use HTTPClientConfig
6. **Alertmanagers**: `notifier/alertmanagerset.go` (line 51) → `config_util.NewClientFromConfig()`

**prometheus-common Bridge**:
- `NewTLSConfig()` - Converts TLSConfig struct to `*crypto/tls.Config`
- `NewClientFromConfig()` - Converts HTTPClientConfig to `*http.Client` with integrated TLS

The answer is saved in `/workspace/answer.json` with complete details on files, symbols, the chain of calls, and a detailed narrative explanation.

The flow works as follows:\\n\\n**1. Configuration Definition (prometheus/prometheus/config/config.go)**\\nPrometheus defines TLS configuration in multiple config structures:\\n- ScrapeConfig (line 747): HTTPClientConfig inline field for scrape targets\\n- RemoteWriteConfig (line 1419): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1434) for remote write endpoints\\n- RemoteReadConfig (line 1587): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1597) for remote read endpoints\\n- AlertmanagerConfig (line 1300): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1305) for alertmanager communication\\n- TracingConfig (line 1160): Direct TLSConfig field (line 1165) for tracing endpoints\\n\\nAll HTTPClientConfig structs (from prometheus-common) contain an embedded TLSConfig field that defines certificates, CA files, server names, and other TLS settings.\\n\\n**2. Scrape Targets (prometheus/prometheus/scrape/scrape.go)**\\nAt line 155 in newScrapeLoop, the scrape client is created from ScrapeConfig.HTTPClientConfig:\\n  client, err := newScrapeClient(cfg.HTTPClientConfig, cfg.JobName, options.HTTPClientOptions...)\\n\\nAt line 2260-2261, newScrapeClient delegates to prometheus-common:\\n  func newScrapeClient(cfg config_util.HTTPClientConfig, name string, ...) (*http.Client, error) {\\n      client, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(cfg, name, optFuncs...)\\n\\n**3. Remote Write/Read Clients (prometheus/prometheus/storage/remote/)**\\nNewWriteClient (client.go line 183) and NewReadClient (client.go line 151) both call config_util.NewClientFromConfig with HTTPClientConfig:\\n  client, err := config_util.NewClientFromConfig(conf.HTTPClientConfig, \\\"remote_storage_write_client\\\", optFuncs...)\\n\\nThe flow starts in storage/remote/write.go (line 169-180) where NewWriteClient is called with ClientConfig containing HTTPClientConfig from RemoteWriteConfig:\\n  c, err := NewWriteClient(name, &ClientConfig{\\n      HTTPClientConfig: rwConf.HTTPClientConfig,\\n      ...\\n  })\\n\\n**4. Some directly use NewTLSConfig:\\n- discovery/triton/triton.go (line 154): tls, err := config.NewTLSConfig(&conf.TLSConfig)\\n- discovery/openstack/openstack.go (line 197): tls, err := config.NewTLSConfig(&conf.TLSConfig)\\n- discovery/aws/ec2.go, discovery/consul/consul.go, discovery/http/http.go and others use HTTPClientConfig\\n\\n**5. Tracing (prometheus/prometheus/tracing/tracing.go)**\\nFor OpenTelemetry tracing, TLSConfig is directly converted at lines 189 and 222:\\n  tlsConf, err := config_util.NewTLSConfig(&tracingCfg.TLSConfig)\\n  \\nThe resulting tls.Config is passed to gRPC credentials (line 193) or OTEL HTTP client options (line 226).\\n\\n**6. (*http.Client, error): Creates an HTTP client by calling NewTLSConfig on the embedded TLSConfig, then configuring the http.Transport with TLS settings, proxy configuration, authentication (basic, bearer, OAuth2), custom headers, and connection timeouts\\n\\n**Architecture Summary**\\nThis design separates concerns: Prometheus defines the config schema and validation logic, while prometheus-common implements the actual TLS/HTTP client creation. This allows for:\\n1. Consistent TLS handling across scrape targets, remote storage, service discovery, and alertmanagers\\n2. SetDirectory() methods on all config types ensure file paths are properly resolved\\n3. Validation of cert/key pairing and file existence\\n4. Clean imports of config_util from prometheus-common with HTTPClientConfig containing TLSConfig\\n5. Configuration changes trigger client reinitialization to pick up new certificates\"",
